           induced reactions on Sm and Pr targets.                A0366  1    4 
AUTHOR     (R.Kossakowski,J.Jastrzebski,P.Rymuza,W.Skulski,       A0366  1    5

INSTITUTE  (3POLIBJ,2FR GRE)                                      A0366  1    7 
REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,32,1612,1985)                                  A0366  1    8 
REL-REF    (M,,J.Bialkowski+,J,NIM,204,91,1982) - The details of  A0366  1    9 
           data acquisition and evaluation                        A0366  1   10 
FACILITY   (CYCLO,2FR GRE) Variable energy cyclotron.             A0366  1   11 
           The typical irradiation time for a beam                A0366  1   12 
           current of 0.3 particle nA was about 2 h. The incident A0366  1   13 
           energy was varied from 71 to 110 MeV for 12C ions and  A0366  1   14 
           from 68 to 120 MeV for 14N ions.                       A0366  1   15 
DETECTOR   (GELI) Three Ge(Li) detectors.                         A0366  1   16 
           (NAICR) 14 NaI(Tl) counters                            A0366  1   17 
MONITOR    The fluorescent K-X-rays of the target atoms have been A0366  1   18 
           used for the cross-section normalization.              A0366  1   19 
ADD-RES    (STRUC,DECAY)                                          A0366  1   20 
           (COMP) Code 'ALICE' (year 1976) and 'LANCELOT' (year   A0366  1   21 
            1985) and gamma-ray multiplicity.                     A0366  1   22 
METHOD     (GSPEC,SITA,ACTIV) Prompt and delayed gamma rays have  A0366  1   23 
           been studied.                                          A0366  1   24 
CORRECTION The correction for the recoil of nuclei from the       A0366  1   25 
           target was applied assuming full momentum transfer     A0366  1   26 
           from the projectile to the compound system. Owing to   A0366  1   27 
           thick targets employed in the present work, this       A0366  1   28 
           correction was small, usually of the order of 10%.     A0366  1   29 
           For the radioactive products having half-lives longer  A0366  1   30 
           than or comparable with the time of measurement, the   A0366  1   31 
           correction for the growth of activity was also made,   A0366  1   32 
           assuming no beam variation during the irradiation of   A0366  1   33 
           the target.                                            A0366  1   34 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-1) Absolute normalization error                   A0366  1   35
